# 自动分配工厂生产：缺什么生产什么。on_daily 对玩家调用。
# 两阶段算法（先算后开，每类每天至多一条线，不重复开线）：
#   阶段1 纯计算：对"今天会开线"的类（首开 / 研出更新型号），需求厂数 = ceil(缺口×单件造价÷400)，
#   顺序分配 min(需求, 剩余空闲)；分完还有剩余 → 全部追加给其中（缺口×造价）最大的类，防止工厂空闲。
#   阶段2 统一开线：每类一条 add_equipment_production，厂数按 30 档细分阶梯落地（requested_factories 不支持变量）。
# 步枪线最先创建（队列最顶、优先分厂）且缺口按至少 10000 把计；飞机只产战斗机和俯冲轰炸机（库存<100 补货）。
# 科技档跟踪 prod_tier_*：研出新型号自动按当前缺口开新档线（引擎无删线效果，旧档线保留可手删）。
# 空闲军工 ≥ 90% 总军工 = 清空队列 → 重置 flag/科技档，重新分配。
# 海军：空闲船坞时按 航母×2→战列×2→轻巡→驱逐 开线（主力舰线引擎上限 5 坞/线，各开两条凑 10 坞），amount=1 产完关线，重开即最新科技。
# MIO：产线制造商两遍择优（专业优先，原型独有 trait / 装备类型识别），无匹配则裸线。
# 由脚本自动生成，勿手改。
auto_production = {
	# ===== 军工分配 =====
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { num_of_available_military_factories > 0.5 } }
		# 清空队列检测：空闲 ≥ 90% 总军工 → 重置产线标记与科技档跟踪，本 tick 重新分配
		set_variable = { prod_total = num_of_military_factories }
		multiply_variable = { prod_total = 0.9 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { num_of_available_military_factories > prod_total } }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_infantry
			set_variable = { prod_tier_infantry = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_support
			set_variable = { prod_tier_support = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_antitank
			set_variable = { prod_tier_antitank = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_antiair
			set_variable = { prod_tier_antiair = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_artillery
			set_variable = { prod_tier_artillery = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_mechanized
			set_variable = { prod_tier_mechanized = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_motorized
			set_variable = { prod_tier_motorized = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_flame
			set_variable = { prod_tier_flame = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_td
			set_variable = { prod_tier_td = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_spg
			set_variable = { prod_tier_spg = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_cas
			set_variable = { prod_tier_cas = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_prod_fighter
			set_variable = { prod_tier_fighter = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { prod_left = num_of_available_military_factories }
		set_variable = { soak_best = 0 }
		set_variable = { soak_pick = 0 }
		# ===== 阶段1：计算各类分配（只算不开） =====
		# --- 步兵装备（单件造价 0.5） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_infantry }
					AND = {
						has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
						check_variable = { prod_tier_infantry < 4 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
						check_variable = { prod_tier_infantry < 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = infantry_weapons1
						check_variable = { prod_tier_infantry < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@infantry_equipment }
			# 前期步枪需求增长快于缺口结算，缺口按至少 10000 把枪计
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit < 10000 } }
				set_variable = { prod_deficit = 10000 }
			}
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 0.5 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 0.5 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_infantry }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 0.5 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 1 }
			}
		}
		# --- 支援装备（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@support_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_support }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@support_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@support_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@support_equipment }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_support > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_support < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_support }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 4 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 2 }
			}
		}
		# --- 反坦克炮（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_tank_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_antitank }
					AND = {
						has_tech = antitank5
						check_variable = { prod_tier_antitank < 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = antitank2
						check_variable = { prod_tier_antitank < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@anti_tank_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@anti_tank_equipment }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_antitank }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 4 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 3 }
			}
		}
		# --- 防空炮（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_air_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_antiair }
					AND = {
						has_tech = antiair5
						check_variable = { prod_tier_antiair < 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = antiair2
						check_variable = { prod_tier_antiair < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_air_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@anti_air_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@anti_air_equipment }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_antiair }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 4 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 4 }
			}
		}
		# --- 火炮（单件造价 3.5） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@artillery_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_artillery }
					AND = {
						has_tech = artillery4
						check_variable = { prod_tier_artillery < 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = artillery1
						check_variable = { prod_tier_artillery < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@artillery_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@artillery_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@artillery_equipment }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 3.5 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 3.5 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_artillery }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 3.5 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 5 }
			}
		}
		# --- 机械化（单件造价 8） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@mechanized_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_mechanized }
					AND = {
						has_tech = mechanised_infantry3
						check_variable = { prod_tier_mechanized < 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = mechanised_infantry2
						check_variable = { prod_tier_mechanized < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@mechanized_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@mechanized_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@mechanized_equipment }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 8 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 8 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_mechanized }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 8 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 6 }
			}
		}
		# --- 摩托化（单件造价 2.5） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@motorized_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_motorized }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@motorized_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@motorized_equipment }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@motorized_equipment }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 2.5 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 2.5 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_motorized }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 2.5 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 7 }
			}
		}
		# --- 喷火坦克（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_flame_chassis > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_flame }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_flame_chassis }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_flame_chassis }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@medium_tank_flame_chassis }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }

			if = {

			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_flame > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = prod_left }
			}
			if = {

			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_flame }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价

				set_variable = { soak_pick = 8 }

		# --- 坦克歼击车（单件造价 15） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_td = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_destroyer_chassis > 0 }

						check_variable = { prod_tier_td < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_destroyer_chassis }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_destroyer_chassis }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@medium_tank_destroyer_chassis }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 15 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 15 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_td = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_td > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_td = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_td < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_td = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_td }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 15 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 9 }
			}
		}
		# --- 自行火炮（单件造价 13） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_spg = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_artillery_chassis > 0 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_spg }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_artillery_chassis }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_artillery_chassis }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@medium_tank_artillery_chassis }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 13 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 13 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_spg = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_spg > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_spg = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_spg < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_spg = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_spg }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 13 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 10 }
			}
		}
		# --- 俯冲轰炸机（单件造价 30，库存阈值 100） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_cas = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_equipment@small_plane_cas_airframe < 100 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_cas }
					AND = {
						has_tech = modern_small_airframe
						check_variable = { prod_tier_cas < 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = improved_small_airframe
						check_variable = { prod_tier_cas < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = 100 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@small_plane_cas_airframe }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 30 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 30 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_cas = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_cas > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_cas = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_cas < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_cas = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_cas }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 30 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 11 }
			}
		}
		# --- 战斗机（单件造价 25，库存阈值 100） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_equipment@small_plane_airframe < 100 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_prod_fighter }
					AND = {
						has_tech = modern_small_airframe
						check_variable = { prod_tier_fighter < 4 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = advanced_small_airframe
						check_variable = { prod_tier_fighter < 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						has_tech = improved_small_airframe
						check_variable = { prod_tier_fighter < 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = 100 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@small_plane_airframe }
			# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 × 单件造价 25 ÷ 400)，400≈单厂3个月IC产出；下限 1
			set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { prod_want = 25 }
			divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
			add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
			round_variable = prod_want
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_want = 1 }
			}
			# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，缺少的装备保底 1 厂
			set_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter = prod_want }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter > prod_left } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter = prod_left }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter < 1 } }
				set_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_fighter }
			# 兜底候选：缺口价值 = 缺口 × 造价
			set_variable = { soak_val = prod_deficit }
			multiply_variable = { soak_val = 25 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_val > soak_best } }
				set_variable = { soak_best = soak_val }
				set_variable = { soak_pick = 12 }
			}
		}
		# ===== 剩余空闲全部追加给今天开线的类中（缺口×造价）最大者 =====
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
				check_variable = { soak_pick > 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 1 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 2 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_support = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 3 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 4 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 5 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 6 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 7 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 8 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 9 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_td = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 10 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_spg = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 11 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_cas = prod_left }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { soak_pick = 12 } }
				add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter = prod_left }
			}
			set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
		}
		# ===== 阶段2：统一开线（每类至多一条） =====
		# --- 步兵装备 ---

			every_military_industrial_organization = {
				limit = {
					is_mio_available = yes

					NOT = { has_mio_equipment_type = armor }

	# ===== 海军：空闲船坞造舰（设计取自 auto_design_equipments） =====
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { num_of_available_naval_factories > 0.5 } }
		# 开线顺序 = 队列优先级：航母×2 → 战列×2 → 轻巡 → 驱逐
		# 主力舰线引擎上限 5 坞/线，故各开两条凑 10 坞
		# --- 航空母舰（5 坞/线，amount=1：每线只造 1 艘，产完自动关线，重开时用当时最新科技） ---
		set_variable = { line_mio = 0 }
		every_military_industrial_organization = {
			limit = { is_mio_available = yes has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_carrier_flight_operations_center }
			ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_tech = advanced_ship_hull_carrier }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_carrier_3 version_name = "1944航空母舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_carrier_3 version_name = "1944航空母舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = improved_ship_hull_carrier }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_carrier_2 version_name = "1940航空母舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_carrier_2 version_name = "1940航空母舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = basic_ship_hull_carrier }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_carrier_1 version_name = "1936航空母舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_carrier_1 version_name = "1936航空母舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 航空母舰（5 坞/线，amount=1：每线只造 1 艘，产完自动关线，重开时用当时最新科技） ---
		set_variable = { line_mio = 0 }
		every_military_industrial_organization = {
			limit = { is_mio_available = yes has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_carrier_flight_operations_center }
			ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_tech = advanced_ship_hull_carrier }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_carrier_3 version_name = "1944航空母舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1

					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {

		else_if = {

				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }

		# --- 战列舰（5 坞/线，amount=1：每线只造 1 艘，产完自动关线，重开时用当时最新科技） ---
		set_variable = { line_mio = 0 }
		every_military_industrial_organization = {
			limit = { is_mio_available = yes has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_super_heavy_shells }
			ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { line_mio < 1 } }
			every_military_industrial_organization = {
				limit = {
					is_mio_available = yes
					OR = {
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_high_speed_raiding
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_heavy_armored_hull
					}
				}
				ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_tech = advanced_ship_hull_heavy }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_4 version_name = "1944重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_4 version_name = "1944重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = improved_ship_hull_heavy }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_3 version_name = "1940重型战舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_3 version_name = "1940重型战舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = basic_ship_hull_heavy }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_2 version_name = "1936重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_2 version_name = "1936重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 战列舰（5 坞/线，amount=1：每线只造 1 艘，产完自动关线，重开时用当时最新科技） ---
		set_variable = { line_mio = 0 }
		every_military_industrial_organization = {
			limit = { is_mio_available = yes has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_super_heavy_shells }
			ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { line_mio < 1 } }
			every_military_industrial_organization = {
				limit = {
					is_mio_available = yes
					OR = {
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_high_speed_raiding
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_heavy_armored_hull
					}
				}
				ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_tech = advanced_ship_hull_heavy }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_4 version_name = "1944重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_4 version_name = "1944重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = improved_ship_hull_heavy }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_3 version_name = "1940重型战舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_3 version_name = "1940重型战舰船体" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = basic_ship_hull_heavy }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_2 version_name = "1936重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_heavy_2 version_name = "1936重型战舰" }
					requested_factories = 5
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 轻巡洋舰（轻炮）（10 坞/线，amount=1：每线只造 1 艘，产完自动关线，重开时用当时最新科技） ---
		set_variable = { line_mio = 0 }
		every_military_industrial_organization = {
			limit = { is_mio_available = yes has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_transom_stern }
			ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { line_mio < 1 } }
			every_military_industrial_organization = {
				limit = {
					is_mio_available = yes
					OR = {
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_super_heavy_shells
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_high_speed_raiding
					}
				}
				ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_tech = improved_ship_hull_cruiser }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_cruiser_3 version_name = "1940轻炮巡洋舰" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_cruiser_3 version_name = "1940轻炮巡洋舰" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = basic_ship_hull_cruiser }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_cruiser_2 version_name = "1936轻炮巡洋" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_cruiser_2 version_name = "1936轻炮巡洋" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 驱逐舰（鱼雷）（10 坞/线，amount=1：每线只造 1 艘，产完自动关线，重开时用当时最新科技） ---
		set_variable = { line_mio = 0 }
		every_military_industrial_organization = {
			limit = { is_mio_available = yes has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_fleet_escorts }
			ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { line_mio < 1 } }
			every_military_industrial_organization = {
				limit = {
					is_mio_available = yes
					OR = {
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_transom_stern
						has_mio_trait = generic_mio_trait_high_speed_raiding
					}
				}
				ROOT = { set_variable = { line_mio = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_tech = advanced_ship_hull_light }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_light_4 version_name = "44雷驱逐" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_light_4 version_name = "44雷驱逐" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = improved_ship_hull_light }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_light_3 version_name = "40鱼雷驱逐" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_light_3 version_name = "40鱼雷驱逐" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = basic_ship_hull_light }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { line_mio > 0 } }
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_light_2 version_name = "鱼雷驱逐36" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
					industrial_manufacturer = line_mio
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = { type = ship_hull_light_2 version_name = "鱼雷驱逐36" }
					requested_factories = 10
					amount = 1
					progress = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
